    SELECT `c0`.`id`, `c0`.`cycle_id`, `c0`.`year`, `t`.`course_id`, `t`.`subject_id`, `t`.`id` AS `id0`, `t`.`name`, `t`.`teacher_id`

) AS `t0` ON `c`.`id` = `t0`.`cycle_id`
